<p><font size="1"> </font></p></div><div style="margin-
left:5.88235294117647%;margin-right:5.88235294117647%;"><hr align="center" 
style='background-color:#000000; border-width:0; color:#000000; height:2pt; 
lineheight:0; width:100%;'></hr><p style="page-break-

<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
&nbsp;
</p>
</div></div><div style="margin-left:10.2941176470588%;margin-
right:10.2941176470588%;"><p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;"><font style="display:inline;font-
weight:bold;">Item 1.01 Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">On August 12, 2016, Gold
Resource Corporation (the &#x201C;Company&#x201D;) acquired all of the 
outstanding shares of Walker Lane Minerals Corporation (&#x201C;WLMC&#x201D;) 
pursuant to a Stock Purchase Agreement dated August 12, 2016 (the 
&#x201C;Purchase Agreement&#x201D;) among the Company and TXAU Development, Ltd.
and TXAU Investment, Ltd., each a privately held Texas limited partnership (the 
&#x201C;Shareholders&#x201D;). Upon completion of the acquisition, WLMC became 
an indirect subsidiary of the Company. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">At the closing, the Company paid
to Shareholders a total purchase price of $13,212,855, consisting of: (i) cash 
in the amount of $152,855 for reimbursement of certain fees incurred during the 
transaction and for maintenance of mining claims, and (ii) 2,000,000 shares of 
the Company&#x2019;s restricted common stock which were valued at $13.1 million 
in the aggregate, based on the closing price of the shares on the NYSE MKT as of
the closing date. The shares are subject to restrictions on resale in accordance
with federal and state securities laws.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">The Purchase Agreement contains 
customary representations, warranties and covenants by the parties. Subject to 
certain limitations and conditions, the Company will be indemnified by the 
Shareholders for damages resulting from breaches or inaccuracies of the 
representations, warranties, and covenants of the Shareholders and WLMC as set 
forth in the Purchase Agreement. The assets held by WLMC consist of certain 
mining claims subject to royalty interests and water rights associated with the 
property located in Mineral County, Nevada. The Purchase Agreement further 
provides that the Company will retain an agreed-upon consultant familiar with 
the property, drill a water well at the property location for development 
purposes, and should the Company determine in the future to abandon any portion 
of the property held by WLMC at the time of the acquisition, it shall transfer 
the affected mining claims to the Shareholders. WLMC has no active operations. 
</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">The foregoing description of the
Purchase Agreement and the transactions contemplated thereby is not complete and
is subject and qualified in its entirety by reference to the text of the 
Purchase Agreement, which is filed as Exhibit 10.1 to this report and 
incorporated by reference in this Item 1.01. The representations and warranties 
of the parties in the Purchase Agreement have been made solely for the benefit 
of the other parties to the Purchase Agreement, and were not intended to be, and
should not be, relied upon by any person other than such parties, including 
shareholders of the Company; should not be treated as categorical statements of 
fact, but rather as a way of allocating risk between the parties; in some cases 
have been qualified by disclosures that were made to the other parties in 
connection with the negotiation of the Purchase Agreement, which disclosures are
not necessarily reflected in the Purchase Agreement; may apply standards of 
materiality in a way that may differ from standards of materiality applied by 
investors; and were made only as of the date of the Purchase Agreement or as of 
such other date or dates as may be specified in the Purchase Agreement, and are 
subject to developments occurring after those dates. </font>
</p>

Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
weight:bold;"></font></p></div><div style="margin-left:10.2941176470588%;margin-

&nbsp;

</div></div><div style="margin-left:10.2941176470588%;margin-
right:10.2941176470588%;"><p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;"><font style="display:inline;font-
weight:bold;">Item 2.01 Completion of Acquisition or Disposition of Assets. 
</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">As described under Item 1.01 of 
this Current Report on Form 8-K, the Company completed its acquisition of WLMC 
effective August 12, 2016 for a total purchase price of $152,855 and 2,000,000 
shares of its common stock. The foregoing does not constitute a complete summary
of the acquisition or the terms of the Purchase Agreement, and reference is made
to the disclosures contained in Item 1.01 hereof and the complete text of the 
Purchase Agreement filed as Exhibit 10.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K, 
which are incorporated by reference herein. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
Unregistered Sales of Equity Securities </font>
<font style="display:inline;font-weight:bold;">Item 3.02
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt;text-indent:36pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">The information set forth in
Item 1.01 of this Current Report on Form 8-K regarding the issuance of the 
2,000,000 shares of common stock by the Company pursuant to the acquisition is 
incorporated herein by reference. The securities issued pursuant to the Purchase
Agreement were offered and sold in private transactions to accredited investors 
(as such term is defined in Rule 501(a), as promulgated under the Securities Act
of 1933), without registration under the Securities Act and the securities laws 
of certain states, in reliance on the exemption provided by Section 4(a)(2) of 
the Securities Act of 1933, as amended and similar exemptions under applicable 
state laws. The securities sold in the foregoing transaction may not be offered 
or sold in the United States absent registration or an applicable exemption from
registration requirements. The Company did not engage in any general 
solicitation or advertising and exercised reasonable care to ensure that the 
purchasers were not underwriters within the meaning of the Securities Act, 
including making reasonable inquiry prior to accepting any subscription, making
written disclosures regarding the restricted nature of the securities and 
placing a legend on the certificates representing the shares.</font>
</p>

Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">

0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">&#x201C;control&#x201D;

<font style="display:inline;">Article 2</font><br /><font

<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">2.1</font><font
style="display:inline;color:#000000;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt

hereof.&nbsp;&nbsp;Shareholders and Company expressly disclaim any warranty not

Company severally and the Shareholders, jointly and severally, represent and 
warrant to Buyer as of the Effective Date (which representations and warranties 
shall survive the Closing for the period as provided in Section 7.1 of this 
Agreement) as follows:</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 72pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-
bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-

<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">(a)</font><font

Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">The Company is a 
corporation duly organized, validly existing and in good standing under the laws
of the State of Nevada. The Company is duly qualified to do business and is in 
good standing in the states where qualification is required due to (i) the 
Company&#x2019;s ownership or lease of real or personal property for use in the 
operation of the Company&#x2019;s business or (ii) the nature of the business 
conducted by the Company. The Company has not at any time owned nor leased any 
real or personal property other than the Property, the Leases or any royalties
described herein, or had any business, operations, obligations or liabilities, 
under any assumed or fictitious names. The Company has all requisite power, 
right and authority to own, operate and lease its properties and assets, and to 
carry on its business as now conducted.</font>

style="display:inline;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Shares</font><font

Date:</font>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 108pt;text-indent: -36pt;font-

<font style="display:inline;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</font>

issued and outstanding capital consists of 54,266,706&nbsp;&nbsp;shares of duly 
authorized and validly issued common stock, which shares are fully paid and non-
assessable and have been issued in compliance with federal and state securities 
laws, and no shares of preferred stock are outstanding, and except as disclosed 
in the SEC Reports, there are no authorized or outstanding warrants, pre-emptive
rights, rights of first refusal or other rights to purchase, or equity or debt

stock of Buyer or any of its subsidiaries.</font>

<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">6.2</font><font
style="display:inline;color:#000000;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">The Shareholders shall prepare, or cause 
to be prepared, and file, or cause to be filed, all tax returns of the Company 
for all periods ending on or prior to the Closing Date and Buyer shall be 
responsible for preparing and filing all tax returns of the Company for periods 
beginning after the Closing Date. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;"></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt;text-align:center;font-
weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">Article 7</font><br /><font
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;">SURVIVAL AND 
INDEMNIFICATION</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 36pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-
bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-
weight:normal;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">7.1</font><font
style="display:inline;color:#000000;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">All representations and warranties of the 
Company and the Shareholders contained in this Agreement or in the Transaction 
Documents or in any certificate delivered pursuant hereto or thereto shall 
survive the Closing for a period of five (5) years from the Closing Date 
(&#x201C;</font><font style="display:inline;font-
weight:bold;color:#000000;">Survival Period</font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">&#x201D;), and such representations and 
warranties shall not be deemed waived or otherwise affected by any investigation
made or any knowledge acquired after Closing Date. The covenants and agreements 
of the Company, the Shareholders and the Buyer contained in this Agreement or in
the Transaction Documents shall survive the Closing.&nbsp;&nbsp;All 
representation and warranties of the Buyer contained in this Agreement or in the
Transaction Documents shall survive for a period of five (5) years from 
Closing.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 36pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-weight:normal;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">7.2</font><font
style="display:inline;color:#000000;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">Subject to the Cap contained in Section 
7.7 below and the parties&#x2019; right to cure under Section 7.4, the 
Shareholders shall indemnify, defend and hold harmless Buyer and the Company 
from and against all claims, damages, losses, liabilities, costs, expenses 
(including, without limitation, settlement costs and any legal, accounting or 
other expenses for investigating or defending any actions or threatened actions 
and any damages or additional tax costs attributable to any reductions in any 
tax attributes of the Company for taxable periods after the Closing Date) 
(&#x201C;</font><font style="display:inline;font-
weight:bold;color:#000000;">Damages</font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">&#x201D;) incurred by the Company prior to
the Closing Date or resulting from: </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 36pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-
indent:-36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-
weight:normal;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 108pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-
bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">(i)</font><font
style="display:inline;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;">any breach by the Company or the 
Shareholders of any representation or warranty in this Agreement or any 
Transaction Document; </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 90pt;text-indent: -27pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 108pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">(ii)</font><font
style="display:inline;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 21.6pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;">any breach of any covenant, agreement
or obligation of the Company or the Shareholders contained in this Agreement or 
any Transaction Document; </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 90pt;text-indent: -27pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 108pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">(iii)</font><font
style="display:inline;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 18pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;">an misrepresentation contained in any statement, 
certificate or schedule furnished by or on behalf of the Company or the 
Shareholders pursuant to this Agreement, the Transaction Documents or in 
connection with</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">the transactions 
contemplated thereby</font><font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">;
&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 90pt;text-indent: -27pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 7pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:7.5pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 108pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">(iv)</font><font
style="display:inline;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 21.6pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;">any state and local income, sales, 
business and occupation, franchise, or other activity-based tax liabilities 
incurred by the Company on or prior to the Closing Date, and any taxes arising 
out of or resulting from the payment of the Purchase Price; or </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 90pt;text-indent: -27pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 108pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">(v)</font><font
style="display:inline;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;">any claims or legal proceedings 
against the Company arising prior to the Closing Date. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 63pt;text-indent: -2.5pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 7pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:7.5pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 7pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:7.5pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 36pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-
bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-
weight:normal;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">7.3</font><font
style="display:inline;color:#000000;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">Subject to the parties&#x2019; right to 
cure under Section 7.4, The Buyer shall indemnify and hold the Shareholders 
harmless from any and all Damages resulting from (i) any breach of any 
representation or warranty made by the Buyer in this Agreement or in any 
Transaction Document and (ii) any breach by the Buyer of any covenant, agreement
or obligation of the Buyer contained in this Agreement or any Transaction 
Document. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 36pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-
weight:normal;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">7.4</font><font
style="display:inline;color:#000000;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">Whenever any claim shall arise for
indemnification under Article 7 of this Agreement, the party seeking 
indemnification (the &#x201C;</font><font style="display:inline;font-
weight:bold;color:#000000;">Indemnified Party</font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">&#x201D;) shall promptly notify the party 
</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;"></font>
</p></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;">
<p><font size="1"> </font></p></div><div style="margin-
left:5.88235294117647%;margin-right:5.88235294117647%;"><hr align="center" 
style='background-color:#000000; border-width:0; color:#000000; height:2pt; 
lineheight:0; width:100%;'></hr><p style="page-break-
after:always">&nbsp;</p></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"></div><div style="margin-
left:5.88235294117647%;margin-right:5.88235294117647%;">
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 36pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9
;text-indent:-36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-
weight:normal;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">from whom
indemnification is sought (the &#x201C;</font><font style="display:inline;font-
weight:bold;color:#000000;">Indemnifying Party</font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">&#x201D;) of the existence of the claim 
and, when known, the facts constituting the basis for such claim. If an 
Indemnifying Party is in </font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">default in the performance of any of the 
other representations, warranties, covenants of or conditions contained in this 
Agreement, the Transaction Documents or any certificate delivered pursuant 
thereto, the Indemnifying Party shall be given the opportunity to cure such 
default within thirty (30) days after notice of such default or if any such 
default is of such nature that it cannot be completely cured within such period,
then </font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">Indemnifying 
Party</font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;"> shall be given an 
opportunity to cure such default if the Indemnifying Party commences such curing
action within thirty (30) days after notice of such default and shall thereafter
diligently and in good faith proceed and continue to cure such default and shall
succeed in curing such default within a reasonable period of time, not to exceed
ninety (90) days.&nbsp; </font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">In 
the event any such claim for indemnification is made resulting from or in 
connection with any claim or legal proceedings by a third party, the notice to 
the Indemnifying Party shall specify, if known, the amount or an estimate of the
amount of the liability arising from such claim. The Indemnified Party shall not
settle or compromise any claim by a third party for which it is entitled to 
indemnification without the prior written consent of the Indemnifying Party, 
which consent shall not unreasonably be withheld, unless suit shall have been 
instituted against it and the Indemnifying Party shall not have taken control of
such suit after notification as provided in Section 7.5 below.&nbsp; </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 36pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-weight:normal;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">7.5</font><font
style="display:inline;color:#000000;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">In connection with any claim giving rise 
to indemnity resulting from or arising out of any claim or legal proceeding by a
person or entity who is not a party to this Agreement, the Indemnifying Party at
its sole cost and expense may, upon written notice to the Indemnified Party, 
assume the defense of any such claim or legal proceeding if it acknowledges to 
the Indemnified Party in writing its obligations to indemnify the Indemnified
Party with respect to all elements of such claim and the Indemnifying Party may 
defend against such claim or litigation, in a manner as it deems appropriate, 
including without limitation, settling such litigation or claim. The Indemnified
Party shall be entitled to participate in (but not control) the defense of any 
such action, with its counsel and at its own expense. If the Indemnifying Party 
does not assume the defense of any such claim or resulting litigation within 
ninety (90) days after the date that notice of such claim is received from the 
Indemnified Party, (a) the Indemnified Party may defend against such claim or 
litigation, in such manner as it may deem appropriate, including, but not 
limited to, settling such claim or litigation, after giving notice of the same 
to the Indemnifying Party, on such terms as the Indemnified Party may deem 
appropriate, and (b) the Indemnifying Party shall be entitled to participate in 
(but not control) the defense of such action, with its counsel and at its own 
expense. If the Indemnifying Party thereafter seeks to question the manner in 
which the Indemnified Party defended such third party claim or the amount or 
nature of any such settlement, the Indemnifying Party shall have the burden to 
prove by a preponderance of the evidence that the Indemnified Party did not 
defend or settle such third party claim in a reasonably prudent manner.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 36pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-
weight:normal;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">7.6</font><font
style="display:inline;color:#000000;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">Notwithstanding anything in this Agreement
to the contrary, the Buyer with the written agreement of the Shareholders may 
set off any amount to which it may be entitled under Article 7 of the Agreement 
against amounts otherwise payable under this Agreement. If the Buyer and 
Shareholders are unable to reach an agreement or settlement as to the 
appropriate amount of a set off within ninety (90) days of the notice provided 
for under Section 7.4, then the parties shall submit such claim to binding 
arbitration.&nbsp; </font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">Such 
arbitration shall be determined and settled by arbitration in the State of 
Nevada by a single arbitrator in </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;"></font>
right:5.88235294117647%;">
</p></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
<p><font size="1"> </font></p></div><div style="margin-
left:5.88235294117647%;margin-right:5.88235294117647%;"><hr align="center" 
style='background-color:#000000; border-width:0; color:#000000; height:2pt; 
lineheight:0; width:100%;'></hr><p style="page-break-
after:always">&nbsp;</p></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"></div><div style="margin-
left:5.88235294117647%;margin-right:5.88235294117647%;">
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 36pt;text-indent:-36pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-weight:normal;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">accordance with 
the Streamlined Arbitration Rules of JAMS. Any arbitrator selected must have 
experience as an arbitrator and specialized knowledge of corporate law.&nbsp; 
</font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">The exercise of such right of
setoff by the Buyer, pursuant to this Section 7.6, will not constitute an event 
of default under this Agreement and will not constitute an election of remedies 
or limit the Buyer in any manner in the enforcement of any other remedies that 
may be available to it in connection with this 
Agreement.&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding the foregoing both parties shall have an 
obligation to take reasonable steps to mitigate any Damages.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 36pt;text-indent: -36pt;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;font-
size:12pt;">7.7</font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;font-
size:12pt;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;text-
indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 0pt;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:12pt;"> Notwithstanding anything in this 
Agreement to the contrary (i) Shareholder shall not be liable to Buyer or 
Company for indemnification to the extent that aggregate amount of Damages is 
less than Twenty Five Thousand and no/100ths Dollars ($25,000.00); and (ii) the 
maximum amount of Damages under this Agreement which Shareholders shall be 
liable for any Damages related to the Shareholders&#x2019; or Company&#x2019;s 
breach of a representation, warranty or covenant to deliver to Buyer good title 
in and to the Mining Claims is the aggregate value of the Purchase Price as 
determined at Closing and for all other indemnification obligations hereunder 
the maximum amount of such Damages for which Shareholder shall be liable in the 
aggregate shall be fifty percent (50%) of the Purchase Price as determined at 
Closing (&#x201C;</font><font style="display:inline;font-weight:bold;font-
size:12pt;">CAP</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:12pt;">&#x201D;).&nbsp;&nbsp;The parties agree that this Cap on Damages 
shall not apply to Damages awarded for actual fraud.</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt;text-align:center;font-
weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">Article 8</font><br /><font
style="display:inline;">notice</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 36pt;text-indent: -36pt;text-

<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">8.1</font><font
style="display:inline;color:#000000;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New

0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">Any notice or other writing, required or 
permitted to be given hereunder, or for the purposes hereof to either party 
shall be sufficiently given if delivered personally, or if sent by prepaid 
registered mail or if by facsimile or e-mail if confirmation of transmission to 
the recipient is received:</font>
</p>

&nbsp;</p>

<td valign="top" style="border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9

<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">9.3</font><font
style="display:inline;color:#000000;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New

style="display:inline;color:#000000;">If any provision of this Agreement is held
to be invalid or unenforceable, then such provision will be fully severable from
this Agreement, and the remaining provisions of this Agreement will remain in 
full force and effect and will not be affected thereby. In lieu of such invalid 
or unenforceable provision, there shall be added automatically as a part of this
Agreement a provision as similar in terms to such invalid or unenforceable 
provision as may be reasonably possible and valid and </font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">enforceable</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">.</font>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 36pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-top:1pt

<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">9.4</font><font
style="display:inline;color:#000000;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">No consent or waiver expressed or implied 
by either party in respect of any breach or default by the other in the 
performance of such other of its obligations hereunder will be deemed or 
construed to be a consent to or a waiver of any other breach or default.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 36pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-weight:normal;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">9.5</font><font
style="display:inline;color:#000000;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">The parties will promptly execute or cause
to be executed all documents, deeds, conveyances and other instruments of 
further assurance which may be reasonably necessary or advisable to carry out 
fully the intent of this Agreement or to record wherever appropriate the 
respective interests from time to time of the parties in the Property.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 36pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:justify;text-

<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">9.6</font><font
style="display:inline;color:#000000;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">This Agreement and any other writing 
delivered pursuant hereto may be executed in any number of counterparts with the
same effect as if all parties to this Agreement or such other writing had signed
the same document and all counterparts will be construed together and will 
constitute one and the same instrument.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 36pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-top:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:justify;text-

<font style="display:inline;color:#000000;">9.7</font><font

Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 25.2pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;color:#000000;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;color:#000000;">Except as otherwise provided herein 
including without limitation as provided in Sections 3.3 and 5.2(h)(v), each 
party to this Agreement shall be responsible for all of its own expenses, legal 
and other professional fees, disbursements, and all other costs incurred in 
connection with the negotiation, preparation, execution, and delivery of this 
Agreement and Transaction Documents and instruments relating hereto and the 
consummation of the transactions contemplated hereby.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt 36pt;text-indent: -36pt;border-top:1pt

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-

ASSETS</font>
<font style="display:inline;font-weight:normal;">LIST OF
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-weight:bold;font-
size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">MINING CLAIMS</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-
size:12pt;">Note:&nbsp;&nbsp;All of the following are unpatented mining claims 
and &#x201C;ownership&#x201D; or &#x201C;possessory title&#x201D; is held 
subject to the paramount title of the United States of America</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:12pt;">A.</font><font
style="display:inline;font-size:12pt;;font-size: 12pt;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt;padding:0pt 36pt 0pt 
0pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;font-size:12pt;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Isabella 
Claims</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:12pt;">Company will
receive a 50% interest in lessees&#x2019; interests in a lease of these claims, 
a 50% ownership in the claims, and a 50% interest in a 6% gross receipts 
production royalty.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<div style="width:100%;"><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"
style="border-collapse:collapse;width: 80.00%;margin-left:0pt;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="border-right:1pt none #D9D9D9 
;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-left:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt

interest in a 6% gross receipts royalty, and a 50% ownership of the subject

in the lease will transfer the benefit of advance royalty payments that have

<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:25.75pt;"><font style="display:inline;">1.</font></font><font style="text-
indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Carr Report</font><font style="display:inline;">. Within 
the limitations imposed on the Carr Report, the report appears to reflect a 
thorough and competent examination of the appropriate records that reflect on 
the title to the Subject</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Claims.</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 6.85pt 0pt 5.85pt;text-indent:36.35pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
Abstract contains notes regarding the transfers in the chain of title to the 
Subject Claims. As a result, the Assessment Abstract is difficult to read and
<font style="display:inline;">We note that the Assessment
decipher. For purposes of this report, we have relied on the written report as 
accurately reflecting what is reflected in the Assessment Abstract. We referred 
to the abstract only to clarify questions arising from our review of the Carr 
Report.</font>

<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-

<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 42pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Requirement</font><font 
style="display:inline;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;None.&nbsp;&nbsp;Advisory Only.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.45pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 6.55pt 0pt 5.85pt;line-height:98.75%;text-
indent:36.15pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:26.95pt;"><font style="display:inline;">2.</font></font><font style="text-
indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">BBU Deeds of Trust</font><font style="display:inline;">. 
Combined Metals Reduction Company ("CMRC") executed a Deed of Trust affecting 
the Subject Claims, dated June 28, 1996, effective as of April 12, 1996, 
recorded on July 31, 1996, in Book 166 OR, page 177, Doc.# 113614, in which 
Chicago Title Insurance Company was listed as the trustee and 
BBU&nbsp;&nbsp;Mezzanine Fund II ("BBU") was listed as the beneficiary (the 
"First BBU Deed of</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Trust").</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 6.65pt 0pt 6.1pt;text-indent:36.15pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">Reciting that it was the trustee
under the June 28, 1996, Deed of Trust, BBU executed a Full Reconveyance of the 
Deed of Trust, dated October 28, 1996, recorded October 30, 1996, in Book 167 
OR, page 426, releasing the First BBU Deed of Trust. The Materials Examined 
contain no substitution of trustee, appointing BBU as the trustee under the 
First BBU Deed of Trust. Under the terms of the deed of trust, BBU had authority
to appoint a new trustee at any time, and it could choose to appoint 
itself&nbsp;&nbsp;as the trustee.&nbsp;&nbsp;BBU's execution of the Reconveyance
suggests that this occurred, but this cannot be confirmed from the 
Materials</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Examined.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.3pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 6.55pt 0pt 6.1pt;text-indent:36.35pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">CMRC executed another Deed of 
Trust affecting the Subject Claims, and naming First American Title Insurance 
Company as trustee and Repadre International Corporation ("Repadre") as
beneficiary, dated effective October 14, 1996, recorded October 30, 1996 in Book
167 OR, page 430, Doc.# 114281 (the "Repadre Deed of Trust").</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.8pt 0pt 6.1pt;text-indent:35.9pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">An additional Deed of Trust, 
affecting the Subject Claims, was executed by CMRC in favor of Chicago Title 
Insurance Company as trustee, and BBU as beneficiary,&nbsp;&nbsp;dated June 28, 
1996, effective as of April 12, 1996, recorded on December, 26, 1996, in Book 
168 OR, page 520, Doc.# 115137 (the "Second BBU Deed of Trust").</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.3pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 6.55pt 0pt 6.1pt;text-indent:36.15pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">Although the First and Second
BBU Deeds of Trust were executed on the same day, have the same effective date, 
are signed by the same individuals, notarized by the same notary, appear to 
secure the same debt, affect the same property, and have the same electronic 
trailer, they are not identical documents.&nbsp;&nbsp;Slight differences in the 
signatures&nbsp;&nbsp;and</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;"></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:3.5pt 5.85pt 0pt 5.35pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;"></font></p></div><div 
style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-right:5.88235294117647%;">
<p><font size="1"> </font></p><div style="width:100%">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
&nbsp;
</p>
</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><hr align="center" style='background-color:#000000; 
border-width:0; color:#000000; height:2pt; lineheight:0; width:100%;'></hr><p 
style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p></div><div style="margin-
left:5.88235294117647%;margin-right:5.88235294117647%;"><div style="width:100%">
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
&nbsp;
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
</p>
<font style="display:inline;">Kelvin J. Buchanan,</font>
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
<font style="display:inline;">March&nbsp;&nbsp;14, 2008</font>
</p>
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
<font style="display:inline;">Page </font><font
style="display:inline;">5</font><font style="display:inline;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;"></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
&nbsp;
</p>
</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><p style="margin:3.5pt 5.85pt 0pt 5.35pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;"><font style="display:inline;">the notary's 
handwriting and signature suggest that the two documents were separately signed 
In addition, the Second BBU Deed of Trust contains a new Article VI entitled 
"Recognition of Repadre Royalty. This Article states that the Second BBU Deed of
Trust is subordinate to an option held by Repadre to acquire a net smelter 
return royalty that is reflected in a Memorandum of Option Agreement between 
CMRC and Repadre, dated October 29, 1996, recorded on October 30, 1996, file No.
114295, in Book 167, page 461 (the "Repadre Option") and that the Deed of Trust 
is subordinate to Repadre's prior rights under the Repadre Deed of Trust.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.3pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 6.05pt 0pt 5.6pt;text-indent:36.05pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">It appears that the Second BBU
Deed of Trust is an altered version of the First BBU Deed of Trust, and that the
alteration occurred several months after the execution&nbsp;&nbsp;of the First 
BBU Deed of Trust. Supposedly, both of the BBU Deeds of Trust were executed and 
acknowledged on June 28, 1996, but the Second BBU Deed of Trust refers to 
recording information relating to the Repadre Option and the Repadre Deed of 
Trust, which information was not known in June of 1996, and could not be known 
until the&nbsp;&nbsp;Memorandum of Option Agreement and the Deed of Trust were
recorded in October of 1996.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 6.1pt 0pt 5.6pt;line-height:98.75%;text-
indent:36.05pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">By Assignment of Deed of Trust,
dated August 13, 1999, recorded May 14, 2004, Doc.# 131033, BBU 
assigned&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Second&nbsp;&nbsp;BBU&nbsp;&nbsp;Deed&nbsp;&n
bsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;Trust&nbsp;&nbsp;to&nbsp;&nbsp;Tesoro&nbsp;&nbsp;Gold Company 
("Tesoro"). By Assignment of Deed of Trust, dated and recorded May 14, 2004, 
Doc.# 131034, Tesoro assigned the Second Deed of Trust to 
Juneau&nbsp;&nbsp;Exploration ("Juneau"). The BBU assignment to Tesoro and the 
Tesoro assignment to Juneau contain recitations similar to those in the Second 
BBU Deed of Trust. Each assignment states that the Second BBU Deed of Trust is 
subordinate to the Repadre Option and the Repadre Deed of Trust.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.3pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.55pt 0pt 5.6pt;text-indent:36.3pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">The Subject Claims were
subsequently sold pursuant to the terms of the Repadre Deed of Trust, and the 
trustee under that instrument executed a Trustee's Deed, dated and recorded on 
May 20, 2004, Doc.# 131124, transferring the Subject Claims to TXAU Investments,
Ltd. ("TXAU"), as the successor to Repadre. Assuming the trustee's sale 
of&nbsp;&nbsp;the claims was regular and conformed with the Repadre Deed of 
Trust and Nevada statutes, the sale served to extinguish all junior interests in
the Subject Claims. Thus, although the purpose of the Second BBU Deed of Trust 
is unclear; because that instrument was junior to the Repadre Deed of Trust, in 
our view whatever rights were created under the Deed of Trust and the subsequent
assignments to Tesoro and Juneau were extinguished when the Subject Claims were 
sold pursuant to the terms of the Repadre Deed of Trust, again assuming that the
sale was properly</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">conducted.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 6.15pt 0pt 6.1pt;text-indent:35.55pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Requirement</font><font style="display:inline;">: You 
should confirm that BBU executed a substitution of trustee appointing itself as 
trustee under the First BBU Deed of Trust and record evidence to that effect in 
Mineral&nbsp;&nbsp;County.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If this 
fact&nbsp;&nbsp;cannot&nbsp;&nbsp;be&nbsp;&nbsp;confirmed,&nbsp;&nbsp;further&nb
sp;&nbsp;analysis&nbsp;&nbsp;should be</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;"></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:3.55pt 6.85pt 0pt 5.95pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:0.95pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt 
none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;"></font></p></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;">
<p><font size="1"> </font></p><div style="width:100%">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
&nbsp;
</p>
</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><hr align="center" style='background-color:#000000; 
border-width:0; color:#000000; height:2pt; lineheight:0; width:100%;'></hr><p 
style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p></div><div style="margin-
left:5.88235294117647%;margin-right:5.88235294117647%;"><div style="width:100%">
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
&nbsp;
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
</p>
<font style="display:inline;">Kelvin J. Buchanan,</font>
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
<font style="display:inline;">March&nbsp;&nbsp;14, 2008</font>
</p>
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
<font style="display:inline;">Page </font><font
style="display:inline;">6</font><font style="display:inline;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;"></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
&nbsp;
</p>
</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><p style="margin:3.55pt 6.85pt 0pt 5.95pt;line-
height:103.75%;text-indent:0.95pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;"><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">undertaken to determine the effect of a beneficiary executing a 
reconveyance, without formally substituting itself as trustee. While such a 
reconveyance might not be technically correct, it would seem that in light of 
estoppel and similar doctrines, the beneficiary would have difficulty 
challenging the effectiveness of the reconveyance. The Second BBU Deed of Trust 
raises some concerns because it appears to be a doctored document and because it
is unclear what its purpose was. Given the unusual nature of the document, you 
may wish to consider examining the procedures used in the trustee's sale under 
the Repadre Deed of Trust to assure yourself that the sale was conducted 
properly and served to extinguish all junior liens.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.35pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.5pt 0pt 7.1pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36.1pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:26.85pt;"><font style="display:inline;">3.</font></font><font style="text-
indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Potential Interests of&nbsp;&nbsp;Repadre</font><font 
style="display:inline;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;CMRC 
and&nbsp;&nbsp;Repadre&nbsp;&nbsp;executed&nbsp;&nbsp;a Memorandum of Offer and 
Subscription Agreement affecting the Subject Claims, effective September 30, 
1996, recorded January 26, 1999, Book 178 OR, 
page&nbsp;&nbsp;725.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Carr Report does not summarize the 
terms&nbsp;&nbsp;of the&nbsp;&nbsp;Agreement.&nbsp;&nbsp;Accordingly, 
we&nbsp;&nbsp;are unable&nbsp;&nbsp;to comment&nbsp;&nbsp;on what impact it 
might have on title to the&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject Claims.&nbsp;&nbsp;Repadre 
subsequently executed an Assignment to TXAU, dated March 30, 2004, recorded on 
April 9, 2004, Doc.# 130697, assigning Repadre's interest in the 
Repadre&nbsp;&nbsp;Deed&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;Trust.&nbsp;&nbsp;Because&nbsp;
&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Agreement&nbsp;&nbsp;is&nbsp;&nbsp;senior to the Repadre 
Deed of Trust, the trustee's sale under the trust deed would not act to 
extinguish any rights&nbsp;&nbsp;Repadre&nbsp;&nbsp;acquired&nbsp;&nbsp;in 
the&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims&nbsp;&nbsp;under&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&n
bsp;prior&nbsp;&nbsp;Agreement. In addition, the Repadre Assignment to TXAU 
refers 
to&nbsp;&nbsp;an&nbsp;&nbsp;unrecorded&nbsp;&nbsp;agreement&nbsp;&nbsp;dated 
March 8, 2004 among Repadre, TXAU and Henry R. Johnston. We assume that TXAU has
satisfied itself that Repadre has 
no&nbsp;&nbsp;remaining&nbsp;&nbsp;interest&nbsp;&nbsp;in 
the&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims and that there&nbsp;&nbsp;are no 
outstanding rights that might have arisen under either the September 30, 
1996&nbsp;&nbsp;Agreement&nbsp;&nbsp;or the March&nbsp;&nbsp;8, 2004</font><font
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Agreement.</font></font>

decoration:underline;">Requirement: </font><font style="display:inline;font-
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-

<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-

decoration:underline;">Possibility of a Senior Lien</font><font 
style="display:inline;">. The 
Title&nbsp;&nbsp;Abstract&nbsp;&nbsp;includes&nbsp;&nbsp;a&nbsp;&nbsp;summary</f
ont><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">of</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">a</font><font
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">Deed of Trust
affecting the Subject Claims, executed by CMRC in favor of First 
American&nbsp;&nbsp;Title Insurance Company, as trustee, and James M. 
Alexander,&nbsp;&nbsp;as beneficiary,&nbsp;&nbsp;dated&nbsp;&nbsp;March 28, 
1994, recorded April 1, 1994, in Book 155 OR, page 610 
(the&nbsp;&nbsp;"Alexander&nbsp;&nbsp;Deed&nbsp;&nbsp;of Trust"). The Title 
Abstract does not describe 
a&nbsp;&nbsp;reconveyance&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Deed&nbsp;&nbs
p;of&nbsp;&nbsp;Trust;&nbsp;&nbsp;however, because the Carr Report does not 
discuss the lien, we have assumed that a reconveyance was recorded. If 
the&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims&nbsp;&nbsp;were&nbsp;&nbsp;not&nbsp;&nb
sp;reconveyed&nbsp;&nbsp;under&nbsp;&nbsp;the Alexander Deed of Trust, the lien 
created pursuant to 
that&nbsp;&nbsp;instrument&nbsp;&nbsp;would&nbsp;&nbsp;have&nbsp;&nbsp;been&nbsp
;&nbsp;senior to the Repadre Deed of Trust and 
would&nbsp;&nbsp;have&nbsp;&nbsp;survived&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;trustee's&nb
sp;&nbsp;sale under&nbsp;&nbsp;the later trust</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">deed.</font></font>

<p style="margin:0pt 5.75pt 0pt 5.85pt;line-height:103.75%;text-

none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New

<font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">6&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</font><font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-
decoration:underline;">Isabella&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims:&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
&nbsp;Notable&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Provisions&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;t
he&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;TXAU&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Lease&nbsp;&nbsp; </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-decoration:underline;">- 
&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-
decoration:underline;">Term and Purchase Option</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">. The 
TXAU&nbsp;&nbsp;Lease&nbsp;&nbsp;provides&nbsp;&nbsp;for&nbsp;&nbsp;a 
production&nbsp;&nbsp;royalty&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;6% of the gross receipts 
received by the lessee 
from&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;sale&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;minerals&nbsp;&nbsp
;from&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Isabella&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims. The 
lease&nbsp;&nbsp;provides&nbsp;&nbsp;for&nbsp;&nbsp;a 
monthly&nbsp;&nbsp;advance&nbsp;&nbsp;minimum&nbsp;&nbsp;royalty&nbsp;&nbsp;paym
ent&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;$1600,&nbsp;&nbsp;which may&nbsp;&nbsp;be offset 
against production&nbsp;&nbsp;royalties&nbsp;&nbsp;otherwise due under the 
lease.&nbsp;&nbsp;The lessee may&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;not assign the lease without 
the consent of the&nbsp; </font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">lessors.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-
bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.55pt 0pt 5.85pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:35.9pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt 
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">The lease was
issued with a perpetual term. For purposes of this Report we have not researched
the enforceability of a perpetual lease; however, we note that a perpetual term 
raises concerns regarding whether the lease is unenforceable as an unreasonable 
restraint on alienation or under similar doctrines.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-
bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.55pt 0pt 5.85pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36.15pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt 
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">Finally, the
lease provides that the lessee has the option to purchase&nbsp;&nbsp;the 
property&nbsp;&nbsp;at&nbsp;&nbsp;any time during the term of the lease; 
however, no 
option&nbsp;&nbsp;price&nbsp;&nbsp;was&nbsp;&nbsp;inserted&nbsp;&nbsp;in&nbsp;&n
bsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;preprinted form. It is unclear whether the option is 
enforceable both because it does not establish a purchase price and because a 
perpetual option may be unenforceable under perpetuities, 
unreasonable&nbsp;&nbsp;restraint&nbsp;&nbsp;on alienation&nbsp;&nbsp;or 
other&nbsp;&nbsp;similar</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">doctrines</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-
bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>

none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-
decoration:underline;">Requirement</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">: Additional analysis of the validity of 
the&nbsp;&nbsp;lease&nbsp;&nbsp;term&nbsp;&nbsp;and&nbsp;&nbsp;purchase 
option&nbsp;&nbsp;should be undertaken&nbsp;&nbsp;or the lease should be amended
to address these&nbsp;&nbsp; </font><font style="display:inline;font-

<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-

decoration:underline;">Isabella Claims: Missing Trust Conveyance. </font><font 
style="display:inline;">By Quitclaim Deed, dated April 12, 1983, recorded on May
5, 1983, in Book 90 OR, page 188, Joe C. Morris and Emma Morris and the Hardrock
Mining Company transferred undivided interests in the Isabella Claims to a 
number of individuals. One of the grantees under the Quitclaim Deed was "William
M. Longhurst, trustee for Caroline Longhurst" (as to a I/8th interest). The 
Materials Examined contain no evidence that Mr. Longhurst conveyed this interest
held in trust to Ms. Longhurst. Nevertheless, Ms. Longhurst subsequently 
executed several documents in the chain of title to the Isabella Claims in her 
own name. The last document in the chain that she executed was the TXAU Lease, 
in favor of CMRC, dated April 1, 1992, a memorandum of which was recorded June 
15, 1992, Book 146 OR, page 978. In executing</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">the</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">lease</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">and</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">the</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">memorandum,</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Ms.</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Longhurst</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font
style="display:inline;">used</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">the</font><font

style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Caroline</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Merrick.</font></font>

</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><p style="margin:3.55pt 6.15pt 0pt 6.35pt;line-
height:103.75%;text-indent:37.45pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;"><font 
style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:20.6pt;"><font 
style="display:inline;">10.</font></font><font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-
left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Isabella&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims:&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
Interest&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Heirs&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;
&nbsp;Suzanne&nbsp;&nbsp;Matkin</font><font 
style="display:inline;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;By&nbsp;&nbsp;Quitclaim Deed, 
dated April&nbsp;&nbsp;12,&nbsp;&nbsp;1983, 
recorded&nbsp;&nbsp;on&nbsp;&nbsp;May&nbsp;&nbsp;5,&nbsp;&nbsp;1983, 
in&nbsp;&nbsp;Book&nbsp;&nbsp;90&nbsp;&nbsp;OR,&nbsp;&nbsp;page 
188,&nbsp;&nbsp;Joe&nbsp;&nbsp;C. 
Morris&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;and&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Emma&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Morris&nbsp;&
nbsp;&nbsp;and&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Hardrock&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;M
ining&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Company transferred&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;undivided 
interests&nbsp;&nbsp;in&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Isabella&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims&nbs
p;&nbsp;to&nbsp;&nbsp;a&nbsp;&nbsp;number&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;individuals, 
including Suzanne Matkin and Sarah D. Narkaus as to an undivided 1/2 
interest.&nbsp;&nbsp;Nevada statutes specify&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;a 
transfer&nbsp;&nbsp;to two&nbsp;&nbsp;or 
more&nbsp;&nbsp;individuals&nbsp;&nbsp;creates&nbsp;&nbsp;a 
tenancy&nbsp;&nbsp;in common, unless&nbsp;&nbsp;a 
different&nbsp;&nbsp;intent&nbsp;&nbsp;is expressed 
in&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;document&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;transfer.&nbsp;&n
bsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Nev.&nbsp;&nbsp;Rev.&nbsp;&nbsp;St.&nbsp;&nbsp;&#xA7; 
111.060.&nbsp;&nbsp;Accordingly,&nbsp;&nbsp;it&nbsp;&nbsp;appears&nbsp;&nbsp;tha
t&nbsp;&nbsp;Ms. Matkin and Ms. Narkaus&nbsp;&nbsp;held their interests 
in&nbsp;&nbsp;the Isabella Claims as tenants&nbsp;&nbsp;in </font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">common.</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 5.4pt 0pt 5.6pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36.95pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt 
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">By</font><font
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">Affidavit</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">of</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">Death and</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">Termination of</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">Joint</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">Tenancy,</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">dated</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">and</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">recorded</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">August 27, 1987, in Book 116 OR, page 
366, Sarah D. Narkaus declared that Suzanne Matkin was deceased and that the 
joint tenancy the two of them held in the Isabella Claims had been terminated by
the death. Joint tenancy is a type of co-ownership in which the interest of a 
joint tenant passes to the other joint tenant immediately upon death. 
Nevada&nbsp;&nbsp;statutes provide that when property is held in joint tenancy, 
the recording of an affidavit of death indicating the death of one of the joint 
tenants raises a presumption that all interest of the deceased in the jointly 
held property has transferred to the surviving joint tenant. Nev. Rev. St. 
&#xA7; 111.365. Nothing in the Materials Examined suggests that Ms. Narkaus and 
Ms. Matkin held their interest in the Isabella Claims as joint tenants. 
Accordingly, the Affidavit of Death does not establish that Ms. Narkaus 
succeeded to Ms. Matkin's interest in the claims.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.2pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-
bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.95pt 0pt 6.8pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none 
#D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-
decoration:underline;">Requirement</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">: You should determine whether Ms. Matkin's estate was probated and 
whether Ms. Narkaus obtained a personal representative's deed as to this 
interest. </font><font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:11pt;">If </font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">so, the deed should be recorded in Mineral County. If the estate was
not probated, a determination of heirship order should be obtained from an 
appropriate court reflecting that Ms. Narkaus was Ms. Matkin's sole heir, and 
the order should be recorded in Mineral County.</font>
</p>

ont><font style="display:inline;">. Subject to other defects noted elsewhere,

these transfers was to transfer a 1/8th ownership interest in the Isabella

<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 6.05pt 0pt 5.6pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36.65pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:21pt;"><font style="display:inline;">12.</font></font><font style="text-
indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Isabella Claims: Spousal Joinder Issues</font><font 
style="display:inline;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Nevada&nbsp;&nbsp;is&nbsp;&nbsp;a 
community&nbsp;&nbsp;property state. A number of conveyances and other transfers
affecting the Isabella Claims&nbsp;&nbsp;were&nbsp;&nbsp;executed by 
individuals, whose marital status is not noted in the Carr Report. If those 
individuals were married at the time of 
the&nbsp;&nbsp;conveyances&nbsp;&nbsp;and&nbsp;&nbsp;if 
their&nbsp;&nbsp;interest&nbsp;&nbsp;in the&nbsp;&nbsp;claims was held as 
community property, the transfers&nbsp;&nbsp;were&nbsp;&nbsp;void&nbsp;&nbsp;or 
voidable&nbsp;&nbsp;under&nbsp;&nbsp;Nevada&nbsp;&nbsp;law.&nbsp;&nbsp;The only 
instrument posing this issue affecting TXAU's leasehold interest 
in&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Isabella Claims is the TXAU Lease itself, under 
which Sarah D. Narkus, Natasha Matkin-Hayes, William Longhurst, John Longhurst, 
Caroline Merrick,&nbsp;&nbsp;Marguerite&nbsp;&nbsp;Cole 
purported&nbsp;&nbsp;to&nbsp;&nbsp;lease the Isabella Claims 
without&nbsp;&nbsp;reciting&nbsp;&nbsp;their marital&nbsp;&nbsp;status or 
joining&nbsp;&nbsp;their </font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font
style="display:inline;">spouse.</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 6.2pt 0pt 5.6pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:35.9pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt 
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">Although the
spousal joinder issues posed by the following documents do not affect TXAU's 
leasehold interest in the 
Isabella&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims,&nbsp;&nbsp;they&nbsp;&nbsp;do&nbsp;&nbsp;affect&nbsp
;&nbsp;Henry&nbsp;&nbsp;R.&nbsp;&nbsp;Johnston's interest in the claims. Prior 
to paying Mr. Johnston any leasehold rentals or royalties, these issues should 
be resolved. The 
following&nbsp;&nbsp;documents&nbsp;&nbsp;pose&nbsp;&nbsp;spousal 
joinder&nbsp;&nbsp;issues affecting&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr. 
Johnston's&nbsp;&nbsp;interest&nbsp;&nbsp;in the&nbsp;&nbsp;Isabella</font><font
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">Claims:</font>

<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-

individuals were married at the time of the conveyance, curative deeds executed

individuals were married at the time the TXAU Lease was executed, a confirmatory
lease executed by both spouses should be obtained and a memorandum of the 
confirmatory lease should be recorded in Mineral County. </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">If </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">the individuals were not married at the 
time of these conveyances or execution of the&nbsp;&nbsp;TXAU Lease or if their 
interest&nbsp;&nbsp;in the Isabella Claims was held&nbsp;&nbsp;as separate

<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-

decoration:underline;">Isabella&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims:&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Isabel
la&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#1&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Claim&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Identified&nbsp;&

aim</font><font style="display:inline;">. A number of documents&nbsp;&nbsp;in 
the chain of title to the Isabella # 1 claim identifies&nbsp;&nbsp;the claim 
as&nbsp;&nbsp;the Isabella Claim; however, according to 
the&nbsp;&nbsp;Carr&nbsp;&nbsp;Report, 
these&nbsp;&nbsp;documents&nbsp;&nbsp;invariably&nbsp;&nbsp;list the correct 
mining&nbsp;&nbsp;claim&nbsp;&nbsp;number&nbsp;&nbsp;assigned&nbsp;&nbsp;by&nbsp
;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;BLM&nbsp;&nbsp;to the&nbsp;&nbsp;Isabella&nbsp;&nbsp;# 1 
claim. Accordingly, we conclude that despite the error in the&nbsp;&nbsp;claim 
name, these documents&nbsp;&nbsp;adequately described the claim and were 
effective to transfer and interest in the Isabella # 1 claim.</font></font>

<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:26.3pt;"><font style="display:inline;">14.</font></font><font style="text-
indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Isabella&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims:&nbsp;&nbsp;Potential&nbsp;&nb
sp;Interest&nbsp;&nbsp;Norsemont&nbsp;&nbsp;Mining&nbsp;&nbsp;Corporation</font>
<font style="display:inline;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Carr Report notes that 
Norsemont Mining Corporation submitted&nbsp;&nbsp;proofs&nbsp;&nbsp;of 
labor&nbsp;&nbsp;on the Isabella Claims for a number of years, but did not 
appear to have a record interest in the&nbsp;&nbsp;claims. Norsemont did execute
a Notice of Termination and Assignment of Interest, dated August 10, 1987, 
recorded on November 22, 1987, in Book 117 OR, page 865, relating to a lease of 
the Isabella Claims to Isabella Partners. Presumably, Norsemont's 
conduct&nbsp;&nbsp;of assessment work on the claims was 
undertaken&nbsp;&nbsp;pursuant&nbsp;&nbsp;to&nbsp;&nbsp;this&nbsp;&nbsp;terminat
ed&nbsp;&nbsp;lease. Accordingly, Norsemont's&nbsp;&nbsp;labor&nbsp;&nbsp;on the
claims does not appear to reflect&nbsp;&nbsp;an adverse 
interest&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;in the</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">claims.</font></font>
</p>
