</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><p style="margin:3.45pt 7pt 0pt 6.55pt;text-
indent:36.9pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;"><font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-
left:0pt; padding-right:20.5pt;"><font 
style="display:inline;">15.</font></font><font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-
left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Isabella and Vulture Dog Claims: Potential Outstanding 
Leases</font><font style="display:inline;">. A Memorandum of Lease and Option to
Purchase, dated April 29, 1983, recorded May 5, 1983, in Book 90 OR, page 198, 
gives notice that Suzanne Matkin, Sarah D. Narkaus, William M. Longhurst, 
Virginia L. Longhurst, Marguerite Longhurst Cole, John Longhurst and Caroline 
Longhurst had given a lease to the Hardrock Mining Company affecting the 
Isabella Claims.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Materials Examined do not reflect a termination 
of the</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">lease.</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.3pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 5.8pt 0pt 6.35pt;text-indent:35.9pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
September 14, 1983, recorded, August 10, 1984, in Book 97 OR, page 950, Minerals
<font style="display:inline;">By Quitclaim Deed, dated
Management, Inc. quitclaimed the Vulture Dog Claims to CMRC. By Assignment also 
dated September 14, 1983, recorded, August&nbsp;&nbsp;10, 1984, 
in&nbsp;&nbsp;Book 97 OR, page 949, Minerals Management, Inc. assigned a lease 
dated July 23, 1982, involving Minoza Mining Joint Venture, Auburn Mining Joint 
Venture, Queen Anne&nbsp;&nbsp;Mining Joint Venture and Beatty Gold Joint 
Venture. It is not clear whether the lease&nbsp;&nbsp;applies to the Vulture Dog
Claims. The Materials Examined do not reflect a termination of the</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">lease.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.3pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 6.95pt 0pt 5.6pt;text-indent:36.85pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Requirement</font><font style="display:inline;">: 
Evidence that the Hardrock lease was terminated should be obtained and recorded 
in Mineral County. You should confirm that the lease involving the various joint
ventures either does not affect the Vulture Dog Claims or, alternatively, obtain
and record evidence in Mineral County that the lease has terminated.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.3pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 6.15pt 0pt 6.55pt;text-indent:37.35pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:21.05pt;"><font style="display:inline;">16.</font></font><font 
style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Soda 5, 46, 47 and 48 Claims: Unsigned Certificates of 
Location</font><font style="display:inline;">. CMRC located the Soda 5, 46, 47 
and 48 on September 18, 1991. No signatures appear on the certificates of 
location for these claims that were recorded in Mineral County and filed with 
BLM. Although certificates of location are typically signed, neither federal or 
state law requires signature. Federal law requires only that the certificate 
contain the name of the locator, the date of location and a description of the 
claim. 30 U.S.C. &#xA7; 28. Similarly, Nevada state law governing the location 
of mining claims requires that the certificate include the name of the claim, 
the name of the locator and his mailing address, the date of location, the 
length and width of the claim and a description of the corners, and a statement 
that a map of the claim has been prepared, which is filed with the certificate. 
Nev. Rev.&nbsp; </font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">St.</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.1pt 7.2pt 0pt 6.8pt;text-indent:0.95pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">&#xA7; 517.050. Accordingly, we
do not believe that the absence of signatures in the certificates affects the 
validity of the claims. You may wish to amend the claims to avoid questions 
being raised about the effect of the absence of signatures.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.3pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 6.3pt 0pt 7.05pt;text-indent:35.9pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Requirement</font><font style="display:inline;">. We do 
not view the absence of signatures on the certificates of location as being 
</font><font style="display:inline;">"fatal" </font><font 
style="display:inline;">to the mining claims involved. In order to avoid a 
potential claim&nbsp;&nbsp;by a rival locater that, as a result of this 
omission, the land covered by these claims remains open to location, you should 
file and record amended certificates of</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">location.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 6.15pt 0pt 7.3pt;line-height:13.7pt;text-
indent:36.6pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:20.8pt;"><font style="display:inline;">17.</font></font><font style="text-
indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Defects in Assessment Work</font><font 
style="display:inline;">. Prior to 1993, the Mining Law required that a claimant
perform assessment work on or for the benefit each mining 
claim.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">To qualify 
as</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;"></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:3.8pt 11.7pt 0pt 10.1pt;line-height:13.6pt;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;"></font></p></div><div 
style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-right:5.88235294117647%;">
<p><font size="1"> </font></p><div style="width:100%">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
&nbsp;
</p>
</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><hr align="center" style='background-color:#000000; 
border-width:0; color:#000000; height:2pt; lineheight:0; width:100%;'></hr><p 
style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p></div><div style="margin-
left:5.88235294117647%;margin-right:5.88235294117647%;"><div style="width:100%">
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
&nbsp;
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
</p>
<font style="display:inline;">Kelvin J. Buchanan,</font>
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
<font style="display:inline;">March&nbsp;&nbsp;14, 2008</font>
</p>
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
<font style="display:inline;">Page </font><font
style="display:inline;">14</font><font style="display:inline;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;"></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
&nbsp;
</p>
</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><p style="margin:3.8pt 11.7pt 0pt 10.1pt;line-
height:13.6pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;"><font 
style="display:inline;">assessment work, work must be "performed in good faith, 
tending to develop the claim and 
directly&nbsp;&nbsp;facilitate&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;extraction&nbsp;&nbsp;o
f&nbsp;&nbsp;minerals&nbsp;&nbsp; </font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">from 
</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">it."2&nbsp;&nbsp;American&nbsp;&nbsp;Law&nbsp;&nbsp;of 
</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Mining &#xA7;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">45.04[5]
[a],</font><font style="display:inline;font-style:italic;">quoting&nbsp; 
</font><font style="display:inline;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Fiske,&nbsp; </font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">"Character 
</font><font 
style="display:inline;">of&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Labor&nbsp;&nbs
p;&nbsp;or&nbsp; </font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Improvements,"&nbsp; </font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;font-
style:italic;">Annual Assessment&nbsp;&nbsp;Work Manual </font><font 
style="display:inline;">2-l , 2-10 (D. Sherwood ed., Rocky Mt. Min. L. 
Fdn.</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">1972).</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:12pt 10.45pt 3pt 0pt;text-indent:36pt;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;font-size:11pt;">It is 
unclear whether enough qualifying work was performed on some of the claims in 
some of the assessment years. In some years, work was conducted that may not 
qualify&nbsp;&nbsp;as assessment work, such as surveying, mapping and assaying.
In one instance no description of the work conducted was included in the 
assessment affidavit. In another instance, an assessment affidavit affecting 
some of the Subject Claims filed in 1988 erroneously stated that the period 
covered was September 1, 1985 to September 1, 1986.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 11.05pt 0pt 10.1pt;line-height:98.75%;text-
indent:35.8pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">Finally, although the Mining Law
allows geological, geochemical or geophysical work as assessment work, the 
statute requires that if such work is relied upon, it be performed by a 
qualified expert and that a detailed report of the work be prepared and filed in
the county. 30 U.S.C. &#xA7; 28-1 (elec. 2007); </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-style:italic;">see also </font><font 
style="display:inline;">43 C.F.R. &#xA7;&#xA7; 3836.12 to .14 (2007). The 
detailed report should describe the names, addresses and professional 
backgrounds of the qualified experts, the location of the work performed, the 
nature, extent and cost of the work and the expert's basic findings. 30 U.S.C. 
&#xA7; 28-1 (elec. 2007); 43 C.F.R. &#xA7; 3836.14 (2007). Geologic and 
geochemical work was conducted on certain of the Subject Claims, but it appears 
that in each instance, either no report was filed or the report that was 
recorded in the county did not satisfy these statutory requirements.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.3pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 11.15pt 0pt 10.6pt;line-height:13.6pt;text-
indent:35.8pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">The Assessment Abstract and Carr
Report reflect that there are defects in the assessment work or filings in the 
assessment years noted below. The work in question or other defect is reflected 
below in italics:</font>
</p>

<p style="margin:0.2pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:3.45pt 10.6pt 0pt 11.55pt;text-indent:35.8pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">The geologic and geochemistry
work appears inadequate because the requirements of 30 U.S.C.A. &#xA7; 28-1 
governing such assessment work were not satisfied. In two years, the work 
conducted on the Vulture Dog claims appears inadequate because no detailed 
report was recorded. In another year, the work conducted on that claim group may
have been inadequate because the report that was filed did not satisfy the 
statutory requirements. Finally, the geochemical work conducted on the Isabella 
claims in the 1982-83 assessment year may have been inadequate because the 
report did not satisfy all of the statutory requirements. We note that in 
several circumstances the affidavits reflecting that geologic work was conducted
also reflect that other qualifying assessment work was performed in those years.
While it possible this other work might suffice to satisfy the annual assessment
work requirement, this cannot be determined with certainty from the Materials 
Examined.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.25pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 10.75pt 0pt 11.8pt;line-height:13.6pt;text-
indent:35.8pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">In addition, sampling, assaying,
geological mapping, and surveying may not be viewed as complying with the 
requirement that assessment work tend to develop the claim </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 10.75pt 0pt 11.8pt;line-height:13.6pt;text-
indent:35.8pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 10.75pt 0pt 11.8pt;line-height:13.6pt;text-
indent:35.8pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 16.15pt 0pt 12.05pt;line-height:105%;text-
indent:0.7pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">1 &nbsp;</font><font
style="display:inline;">It is not clear from the Carr Report what claims were 
included in this affidavit; however, it appears that this defect 
affected&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Soda claims.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 10.75pt 0pt 11.8pt;line-height:13.6pt;text-
indent:35.8pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 10.75pt 0pt 11.8pt;line-height:13.6pt;text-
indent:35.8pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;"></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 10.75pt 0pt 0pt;line-height:13.6pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;"></font></p></div><div 
style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-right:5.88235294117647%;">
<p><font size="1"> </font></p><div style="width:100%">
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
&nbsp;
</p>
</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><hr align="center" style='background-color:#000000; 
border-width:0; color:#000000; height:2pt; lineheight:0; width:100%;'></hr><p 
style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p></div><div style="margin-
left:5.88235294117647%;margin-right:5.88235294117647%;"><div style="width:100%">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
&nbsp;
</p>
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
<font style="display:inline;">Kelvin J. Buchanan,</font>
</p>
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
<font style="display:inline;">March&nbsp;&nbsp;14, 2008</font>
</p>
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
<font style="display:inline;">Page </font><font
style="display:inline;">16</font><font style="display:inline;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;"></font>
</p>
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
&nbsp;
</p>
</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><p style="margin:0.05pt 10.75pt 0pt 0pt;line-
height:13.6pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;"><font style="display:inline;">and 
facilitate the extraction of minerals from it. In each of the years in which 
this kind of work was recited as having been performed, other activities are 
recited as having been conducted that do appear to satisfy this requirement. 
Although it is possible that this latter type of work would be sufficient to 
satisfy the annual work requirement, this cannot be determined with certainty 
from the Materials Examined.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.5pt 0pt 5.55pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36.2pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt 
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">These defects
might indicate that the usual presumption attendant to a filing of an affidavit 
of labor that adequate assessment work was done may not be available for the 
relevant assessment years. However, proof that proper assessment work was 
performed in the pertinent assessment year can be established by other evidence,
if such evidence exists. </font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">If </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">proper assessment work was not in fact 
performed during the years noted above, land included within the affected claims
was open to location by rival claimants until qualifying assessment work was 
resumed. Because the Carr Report does not include a conflicting claims analysis,
it is unclear whether a rival claimant could argue because of the defective 
assessment work, his claims are senior to the affected Subject Claims.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-
bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.4pt 0pt 5.55pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36.2pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt 
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">In addition,
under current BLM regulations, failure to comply substantially with assessment 
work requirements can lead to claim forfeiture where the land is withdrawn from
mineral entry or the mineral for which the claim was located is no longer 
subject to the Mining Law. 43 C.F.R. &#xA7; 3836.15. We note that in the past 
BLM did not limit its authority to cancel a claim for failure to substantially 
comply with assessment work requirements to situations in which the land is 
withdrawn of the mineral being no longer subject to the Mining Law. Previous 
regulations provided that failure to "comply substantially with the requirements
of an annual expenditure of $100 in labor or improvements . . . will render the 
claim subject to cancellation." 43 C.F.R. &#xA7; 3851.3(a) (2003). It is 
possible that in the future, the agency could again adopt this more aggressive 
policy.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-
bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.3pt 0pt 5.55pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36.2pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt 
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-
decoration:underline;">Requirement</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">: A claim conflict analysis should be undertaken to insure that no 
rival claimants over staked the land 
covered&nbsp;&nbsp;by&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;affected&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject&nbsp
;&nbsp;Claims&nbsp;&nbsp;during&nbsp;&nbsp;the periods that questionable 
assessment work 
was&nbsp;&nbsp;performed.&nbsp;&nbsp;We&nbsp;&nbsp;are&nbsp;&nbsp;aware&nbsp;&nb
sp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;no&nbsp;&nbsp;authority&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;would 
indicate that the possible deficiencies noted above 
are&nbsp;&nbsp;such&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;"substantial compliance" with the
assessment work requirements has not been achieved or that would support the use
of the cancellation&nbsp;&nbsp;proceedings&nbsp;&nbsp;noted&nbsp;&nbsp;above to 
cancel claims for these types&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of irregularities. However, to 
avoid&nbsp;&nbsp;any&nbsp;&nbsp;possibility&nbsp;&nbsp;of 
cancellation&nbsp;&nbsp;proceedings,&nbsp;&nbsp;you&nbsp;&nbsp;may wish to 
consider relocating the affected claims.&nbsp;&nbsp;Prior to 
doing&nbsp;&nbsp;so, however, we recommend&nbsp;&nbsp;that a careful claim 
conflict analysis be conducted to determine whether conflicting 
claims&nbsp;&nbsp;affect the land. </font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">If</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">they </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">do, additional consideration should be 
given to whether relocation is prudent.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.35pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.6pt 0pt 5.8pt;line-height:102.92%;text-
indent:37.2pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:20.6pt;"><font style="display:inline;">18.</font></font><font style="text-
indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Defects&nbsp;&nbsp;in&nbsp;&nbsp;Notice&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbs
p;&nbsp;Intent&nbsp;&nbsp;to&nbsp;&nbsp;Hold</font><font 
style="display:inline;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The&nbsp;&nbsp;Carr&nbsp;&nbsp;Report
&nbsp;&nbsp;notes&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;Notices of Intent 
filed&nbsp;&nbsp;on&nbsp;&nbsp;some&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Subj
ect&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims&nbsp;&nbsp;in&nbsp;&nbsp;both&nbsp;&nbsp;2003&nbsp;&nbsp;a
nd&nbsp;&nbsp;2004&nbsp;&nbsp;state that&nbsp;&nbsp;the claimant</font></font>
</p>
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.2pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;"></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:3.55pt 6.65pt 0pt 5.55pt;line-height:103.75%;text-

Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;"><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">intends to hold the claims for the 2003-04 assessment year. No 
Notice of Intent appears of record&nbsp;&nbsp;stating that the 
claimant&nbsp;&nbsp;intends to 
hold&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;claim&nbsp;&nbsp;for the&nbsp;&nbsp;2004-
05&nbsp;&nbsp;assessment&nbsp;&nbsp;year.&nbsp;&nbsp;It is not clear which 
claims are being&nbsp;&nbsp;referred&nbsp;&nbsp;to, but&nbsp;&nbsp;it appears 
that the&nbsp;&nbsp;comment relates to&nbsp;&nbsp;the Soda claims. At most, this
irregularity suggests that the usual presumption&nbsp;&nbsp;attendant to filing 
a notice of intent to hold that the claimant did intend to hold the claims may 
not be available for the relevant 
assessment&nbsp;&nbsp;years.&nbsp;&nbsp;However,&nbsp;&nbsp;because&nbsp;&nbsp;t
he intent to hold&nbsp;&nbsp;can readily be established by proof of the payment 
of the 
maintenance&nbsp;&nbsp;fees&nbsp;&nbsp;for&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;year,&nbsp
;&nbsp;we&nbsp;&nbsp;do&nbsp;&nbsp;not view this irregularity&nbsp;&nbsp;as 
affecting the validity&nbsp;&nbsp;of the </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">claims.</font>

<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-

</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.9pt 0pt 6.05pt;line-height:105%;text-

<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:20.6pt;"><font style="display:inline;">19.</font></font><font style="text-
indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Examination of the Soda #32- to #35</font><font 
style="display:inline;">. We note that although the Soda #32-</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">to #35 claims
are included in the Carr Report, the Certificate Abstract does not include a 
summary of the Certificates for these claims. Reference to these claims do 
appear in Assessment</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Abstract,</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">suggesting</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font
style="display:inline;">that</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Mr.</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Carr</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">did</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">include</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">the</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">claims</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">in</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">his</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">title</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">review.</font></font>

<p style="margin:0.3pt 0pt 0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 6.3pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none 
#D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-
decoration:underline;">Requirement</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">: You should confirm that Mr. 
Carr&nbsp;&nbsp;did&nbsp;&nbsp;include&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;claims&nbsp;&nb
sp;in&nbsp;&nbsp;his&nbsp;&nbsp;review and did review the Certificates of 
location 
for&nbsp;&nbsp;these&nbsp;&nbsp;claims&nbsp;&nbsp;to&nbsp;&nbsp;assure&nbsp;&nbs
p;that&nbsp;&nbsp;they&nbsp;&nbsp;comply&nbsp;&nbsp;with all statutory 
</font><font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">requirements.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 5.9pt 0pt 6.55pt;line-height:105%;text-

<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:21.8pt;"><font style="display:inline;">20.</font></font><font style="text-
indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Vulture Dog #16: Missing Case File: </font><font 
style="display:inline;">The Carr Report reflects that BLM could not locate the 
case file for the Vulture Dog #16 on the date of Mr. Carr's review and, 
accordingly, he was unable to ascertain the date upon which the Certificate of 
Location was filed with the</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">BLM.</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.8pt 0pt 6.55pt;line-height:105.83%;text-
indent:36.2pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt 
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New

<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-
decoration:underline;">Requirement:</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="font-size:11pt;border-bottom-
style:solid;border-bottom-width:2pt;height:100%;text-
indent:0pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">Additional inquiry should be made to ensure that the Certificate of 
Location for this claim was timely filed with the BLM. </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">If
</font><font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">it was not, the claim should
be relocated.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.5pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.2pt 0pt 6.55pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36.25pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:22pt;"><font style="display:inline;">21.</font></font><font style="text-
indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Isabella # 1 to #3: Descriptions Defects</font><font 
style="display:inline;">. The Certificate Abstract indicates that the 
certificates of location for the Isabella # 1 to #3 claims contain mistakes in 
the descriptions of the claims. The notation is not clear as to what the mistake
is, except that it appears to be mistakes in the calls to the corners of the 
claims. Federal and&nbsp;&nbsp;state law</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">require that 
certificates of location describe the location of the claims with reference to a
natural object or permanent monument. The abstract indicates that, as required 
by state and federal law, a map of the claims was recorded in the county and 
filed with BLM. </font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">If</font><font style="display:inline;">when 
</font><font style="display:inline;">read in light of the map, the Certificate 
is clear as to where the claims are located, we do</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">not believe 
the mistake in</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">the description would be fatal to the 
claims.</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.2pt 0pt 0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.6pt 0pt 6.75pt;line-height:103.75%;text-

none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-

Certificates&nbsp;&nbsp;and&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;mining&nbsp;&nbsp;claim&nb
sp;&nbsp;map should be undertaken to ascertain whether 
the&nbsp;&nbsp;Certificates&nbsp;&nbsp;clearly&nbsp;&nbsp;depict&nbsp;&nbsp;the&
nbsp;&nbsp;location&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;these claims. </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
size:11pt;">If</font><font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">they 
</font><font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">do, amended certificates of 
location and maps should be prepared and
recorded&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;in&nbsp;&nbsp;Mineral&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;County&nbsp;&nb
sp;&nbsp;and&nbsp;&nbsp;filed&nbsp;&nbsp;with&nbsp;&nbsp;BLM&nbsp;&nbsp;in&nbsp;

sp;&nbsp;in&nbsp;&nbsp; </font><font style="display:inline;font-

</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>

<font style="display:inline;font-

</p>
<font style="display:inline;">March&nbsp;&nbsp;14, 2008</font>

<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-

</p>

<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
&nbsp;
</p>
</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><p style="margin:3.55pt 6.75pt 0pt 6.35pt;line-
height:105%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt 
none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;"><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">Certificates. </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">If </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">it is concluded that the Certificates do 
not clearly depict the location of the claims, the claims should be 
relocated.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.5pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 6.5pt 0pt 6.15pt;line-height:102.92%;text-
indent:36.15pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:21.7pt;"><font style="display:inline;">22.</font></font><font style="text-
indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Failure to Identify Quarter Sections</font><font 
style="display:inline;">. The 
Assessment&nbsp;&nbsp;Abstract&nbsp;&nbsp;indicates 
that&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;certificates&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;location&nb
sp;&nbsp;for&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Isabella&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims,&nbsp;&nbsp;th
e&nbsp;&nbsp;Vulture&nbsp;&nbsp;Dog&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims,&nbsp;&nbsp;and 
the</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Soda</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 6.5pt 0pt 6.15pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">#37 and #38
claims do not describe the quarter sections in which the claims are located, as 
required by federal regulations. 43&nbsp;&nbsp;C.F.R.&nbsp;&nbsp;&#xA7; 
3832.12.&nbsp;&nbsp;However,&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Carr 
Report&nbsp;&nbsp;indicates that the maps that were filed with the claims 
supplied this missing 
information.&nbsp;&nbsp;We&nbsp;&nbsp;concur&nbsp;&nbsp;that including the 
quarter section location on the claim maps was sufficient to satisfy the 
regulatory </font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">requirement.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-
bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 42.3pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9
;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
decoration:underline;">Requirement</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">:&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;None.&nbsp;&nbsp;Advisory only.</font>
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-
</p>
<p style="margin:0.3pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 6.15pt 0pt 6.35pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:35.95pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:21.95pt;"><font style="display:inline;">23.</font></font><font 
style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Vulture Dog #22: Possible Failure to File Map</font><font
style="display:inline;">. The Assessment Abstract contains a column labeled 
</font><font style="display:inline;">"NRS </font><font 
style="display:inline;">517.040." We assume that this column reflects whether a 
claim</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">map</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">was</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">recorded</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">in</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Mineral</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">County</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">as</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">required</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">by</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Nev.</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">Rev.</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">St.</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&#xA7;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">517.040</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">and</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">filed with 
BLM as required by federal regulation. 43 C.F.R. &#xA7; 3832.12. The notes 
indicate that no map was filed for the Vulture Dog #22. Because the Carr Report 
does not note this omission,</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">it</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">may 
be</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">that</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">the</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">handwritten 
notation</font><font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font
decoration:underline;">Requirement</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">: It should be&nbsp;&nbsp;confirmed&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;a 
map&nbsp;&nbsp;was&nbsp;&nbsp;filed for this claim.&nbsp; </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:11pt;">If
</font><font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">it was not, additional 
analysis should be undertaken to determine whether the claim should be 
relocated&nbsp;&nbsp;or whether the omission can be cured 
by&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;amendment.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
style="display:inline;">was</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">made</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">in</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">error.</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.35pt 0pt 0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9
;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 6.4pt 0pt 6.6pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:35.9pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt 
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.8pt 0pt 6.35pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36.2pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:21.95pt;"><font style="display:inline;">24.</font></font><font 
style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Maintenance Fee Filings</font><font 
style="display:inline;">. The Carr 
Report&nbsp;&nbsp;notes&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;&nbsp;Carr&nbsp;&nbs
p;did&nbsp;&nbsp;not&nbsp;&nbsp;review the maintenance fee payment for the 
Subject Claims for the 2007-2008 maintenance year, because you had 
assured&nbsp;&nbsp;yourself&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;they&nbsp;&nbsp;were 
timely&nbsp;&nbsp;paid.&nbsp;&nbsp;The report&nbsp;&nbsp;also&nbsp;&nbsp;notes 
that his examination of the county 
records&nbsp;&nbsp;inadvertently&nbsp;&nbsp;did 
not&nbsp;&nbsp;include&nbsp;&nbsp;an examination&nbsp;&nbsp;of the Notices of 
Intent to Hold the Subject Claims recorded for the 1999-2000 to 2006-2007 
period.</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.7pt 0pt 6.35pt;line-height:105%;text-

none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-
decoration:underline;">Requirement</font><font style="display:inline;font-

Hold&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims&nbsp;&nbsp;for 
the&nbsp;&nbsp;1999-2000&nbsp;&nbsp;to 2006-2007 period should be reviewed to 
assess&nbsp;&nbsp;whether&nbsp;&nbsp;they&nbsp;&nbsp;comply&nbsp;&nbsp;with&nbsp
;&nbsp;Nevada statutes. The maintenance 
fee&nbsp;&nbsp;payments&nbsp;&nbsp;filed&nbsp;&nbsp;with&nbsp;&nbsp;BLM&nbsp;&nb
sp;for&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;2007-2008&nbsp;&nbsp;maintenance 
year&nbsp;&nbsp;should be reviewed to assess whether&nbsp;&nbsp;it 
complied&nbsp;&nbsp;with federal </font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;font-

<p style="margin:0.25pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-

<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-

style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Areas Closed to Mineral Entry</font><font 
style="display:inline;">. The Carr Report notes a 400&nbsp;&nbsp;foot 
highway&nbsp;&nbsp;right of way and a material site affect land included within 
the&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims.&nbsp;&nbsp;Attached&nbsp;&nbsp;to the 
report is a serial register page for the material site right of way, which 
indicates that the material site was issued under the 
Federal&nbsp;&nbsp;Highway&nbsp;&nbsp;Act&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;1921.&nbsp;&n
bsp;Material&nbsp;&nbsp;sites&nbsp;&nbsp;issued&nbsp;&nbsp;under that Act are 
closed to mineral 
entry.&nbsp;&nbsp;The&nbsp;&nbsp;report&nbsp;&nbsp;does&nbsp;&nbsp;not&nbsp;&nbs
p;indicate&nbsp;&nbsp;under&nbsp;&nbsp;what&nbsp;&nbsp;authority the highway 
right of way was issued; however, it is possible that the land 
encompassed&nbsp;&nbsp;within&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;right&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbs
p;&nbsp;way&nbsp;&nbsp;is&nbsp;&nbsp;similarly&nbsp;&nbsp;closed&nbsp;&nbsp;to&n
bsp;&nbsp;mineral&nbsp;&nbsp;entry.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;To&nbsp;&nbsp;the</font><fo
nt style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">extent</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>

<font style="display:inline;font-

</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><p style="margin:3.55pt 6.7pt 0pt 5.85pt;line-
height:103.75%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt
none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;"><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">that an otherwise valid unpatented mining
claim overlaps onto land that is closed to entry, the claim is void as to the 
area of overlap. In the event the point of discovery for an unpatented mining 
claim is on land closed to entry, the claim is void in its entirety and any 
public land included within the claim is open for location.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-

11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 7.3pt 0pt 6.55pt;line-height:105%;text-
indent:35.5pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt 
none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-
decoration:underline;">Requirement:</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;"> You should assure 
yourself&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;points&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nb
sp;discovery&nbsp;&nbsp;for&nbsp;&nbsp;the Subject Claims&nbsp;&nbsp;are located
on open public&nbsp;&nbsp;domain&nbsp;&nbsp;land.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.55pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 6.1pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36.25pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:28.15pt;"><font style="display:inline;">26.</font></font><font 
style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Conflicts With Senior Unpatented Claims</font><font 
style="display:inline;">. 
It&nbsp;&nbsp;appears&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;in&nbsp;&nbsp;preparing&nbsp;&n
bsp;the Carr Report Mr. Carr did&nbsp;&nbsp;not perform&nbsp;&nbsp;a 
claim&nbsp;&nbsp;conflict&nbsp;&nbsp;analysis&nbsp;&nbsp;of 
the&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims.&nbsp;&nbsp;To the extent that an 
otherwise valid unpatented mining claim overlaps onto 
patented&nbsp;&nbsp;land&nbsp;&nbsp;or valid, senior unpatented claims, the 
claim is void as to the area of overlap.&nbsp;&nbsp;In the&nbsp;&nbsp;event the 
point of discovery for an unpatented mining claim is on patented land or land 
included&nbsp;&nbsp;in a valid senior claim, the claim is void in its entirety 
and any public&nbsp;&nbsp;land included within 
the&nbsp;&nbsp;claim&nbsp;&nbsp;is open for</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">location.</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 6.6pt 0pt 6.35pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none 
#D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-
decoration:underline;">Requirement</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">: A qualified draftsman or engineer should plot the Subject Claims 
and all of the potentially conflicting claims in the area. You should then 
assure yourself that none of the points of discovery are located on patented 
land or senior valid claims.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.2pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 6.3pt 0pt 6.1pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36.25pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:22.05pt;"><font style="display:inline;">27.</font></font><font 
style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Multiple Surface Use Act of 1955</font><font 
style="display:inline;">. The Subject Claims were</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display:inline;">located after
passage of the Multiple Surface Use Act of 1955, 30 U.S.C. &#xA7; 601. Pursuant 
to this Act, the surface rights associated with an unpatented mining claim are
subject to the&nbsp;&nbsp;rights&nbsp;&nbsp;of the United States to manage and 
dispose&nbsp;&nbsp;of 
the&nbsp;&nbsp;vegetative&nbsp;&nbsp;and&nbsp;&nbsp;other&nbsp;&nbsp;surface 
resources,&nbsp;&nbsp;and to use the surface or to authorize others (including 
the general public) to traverse or to use the surface in a manner that does not 
unreasonably interfere&nbsp;&nbsp;with&nbsp;&nbsp;legitimate 
mining&nbsp;&nbsp;operations.&nbsp;&nbsp;As a result, the surface of the Subject
Claims may&nbsp;&nbsp;be&nbsp;&nbsp;subject to&nbsp;&nbsp;existing&nbsp;&nbsp;or
future&nbsp;&nbsp;surface uses by third </font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">parties.</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 6.35pt 0pt 6.55pt;line-height:105%;text-
indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none 
#D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;text-
decoration:underline;">Requirement:</font><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;"> None, advisory only. Operations on the Subject Claims should be 
conducted with due regard for the rights of authorized conflicting uses of 
federal land.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 42.8pt;text-indent: -36.2pt;text-
decoration:underline;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:-36.2pt; padding-
right:25.25pt;"><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:none;">E.</font></font><font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; 
padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:none;"></font><font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">COMMENTS 
AND</font><font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">QUALIFICATIONS</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.25pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 5.8pt 0pt 6.35pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:37.45pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:25.8pt;"><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11.5pt;">1.</font></font><font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; 
padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11.5pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Discovery;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Physical&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Act
s&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Location</font><font 
style="display:inline;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;An&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp
;unpatented&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;mmmg&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;claim is 
created&nbsp;&nbsp;by&nbsp;&nbsp;performing&nbsp;&nbsp;certain&nbsp;&nbsp;acts&n
bsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;location&nbsp;&nbsp;on the&nbsp;&nbsp;ground&nbsp;&nbsp;
(e.g.,&nbsp;&nbsp;erection&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;a discovery monument, 
marking of boundaries), making a "discovery" of a valuable mineral deposit (as 
defined in the 
general&nbsp;&nbsp;mining&nbsp;&nbsp;law)&nbsp;&nbsp;within&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;
&nbsp;boundaries&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;claim,&nbsp;&nbsp;and
filing&nbsp;&nbsp;and 
recording&nbsp;&nbsp;evidence&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;existence&
nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;claim.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;An&nbsp;&n
bsp;unpatented&nbsp;&nbsp;mining claim,&nbsp;&nbsp;although 
properly&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;filed&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;and&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;recorded,&
nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;is&nbsp;&nbsp;not&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;valid&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;until
&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;locater&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;has&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;m
ade a&nbsp;&nbsp;discovery&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;and 
performed&nbsp;&nbsp;such&nbsp;&nbsp;physical&nbsp;&nbsp;acts.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
&nbsp;Determination&nbsp;&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;whether&nbsp;&nbsp;a&nbsp;&nbsp;dis
covery has occurred or the physical acts of location have been performed on the 
ground are determinations&nbsp;&nbsp;that </font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">are</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.2pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;"></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:3.55pt 6.8pt 0pt 5.35pt;line-height:105%;text-
indent:0.2pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;"></font></p></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;">
<p><font size="1"> </font></p><div style="width:100%">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
&nbsp;
</p>
</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><hr align="center" style='background-color:#000000; 
border-width:0; color:#000000; height:2pt; lineheight:0; width:100%;'></hr><p 
style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p></div><div style="margin-
left:5.88235294117647%;margin-right:5.88235294117647%;"><div style="width:100%">
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
&nbsp;
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
</p>
<font style="display:inline;">Kelvin J. Buchanan,</font>
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
<font style="display:inline;">March&nbsp;&nbsp;14, 2008</font>
</p>
size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
<font style="display:inline;">Page </font><font
style="display:inline;">20</font><font style="display:inline;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;"></font><font style="display:inline;"></font><font 
style="display:inline;"></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 12pt;">
&nbsp;
</p>
</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.88235294117647%;margin-
right:5.88235294117647%;"><p style="margin:3.55pt 6.8pt 0pt 5.35pt;line-
height:105%;text-indent:0.2pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;"><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11pt;">beyond the scope of this report. We therefore express no opinion as 
to the validity of any of the Subject Claims in this respect.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.55pt 0pt 0pt;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 7.15pt 0pt 5.8pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times 
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:27.3pt;"><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11.5pt;">2.</font></font><font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; 
padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11.5pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Lode vs. Placer Location</font><font 
style="display:inline;">. Federal and state laws and regulations distinguish 
between lode and placer deposits by providing similar but&nbsp;&nbsp;separate 
procedures&nbsp;&nbsp;for locating each type of claim. While it is often 
difficult to determine whether a deposit should be characterized as a lode or 
placer,&nbsp;&nbsp;the difference&nbsp;&nbsp;is critical to the 
validity&nbsp;&nbsp;of the&nbsp;&nbsp;claims,&nbsp;&nbsp;for&nbsp;&nbsp;use of 
the wrong type of location will result in an 
invalid&nbsp;&nbsp;location.&nbsp;&nbsp;The 
Materials&nbsp;&nbsp;Examined&nbsp;&nbsp;do not reflect whether the Certificates
of Location describe the claims as lodes or placers. Determination as to whether
the various areas of mineralization upon which&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject
Claims were located are properly characterized as lode or placer deposits is a 
geologic determination&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;is 
beyond&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;scope of our</font><font 
style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font><font 
style="display:inline;">examination.</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 6.1pt 0pt 6.05pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36.25pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times
New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; padding-
right:26.8pt;"><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11.5pt;">3.</font></font><font style="text-indent:0pt;margin-left:0pt; 
padding-right:4pt;text-align:left"><font style="display:inline;font-
size:11.5pt;"></font><font style="display:inline;text-
decoration:underline;">Assessment Work</font><font style="display:inline;">. As 
noted above, we did not review in detail Mr. Carr's handwritten notes regarding 
the annual 
assessment&nbsp;&nbsp;work&nbsp;&nbsp;filings&nbsp;&nbsp;made&nbsp;&nbsp;on&nbsp
;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject&nbsp;&nbsp;Claims. We did however, review the type
of work that&nbsp;&nbsp;was&nbsp;&nbsp;performed&nbsp;&nbsp;and 
noted&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;in&nbsp;&nbsp;every assessment year for which 
work was 
required,&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;work&nbsp;&nbsp;was&nbsp;&nbsp;performed&nbs
p;&nbsp;on&nbsp;&nbsp;one&nbsp;&nbsp;or more contiguous claims for the benefit 
of a group of claims. The use of this type of work, commonly called "group 
assessment work", 
is&nbsp;&nbsp;permissible&nbsp;&nbsp;under&nbsp;&nbsp;the&nbsp;&nbsp;general&nbs
p;&nbsp;mining&nbsp;&nbsp;law. The test under federal mining law for whether 
work performed outside the boundaries of a&nbsp;&nbsp;claim (whether or not on a
contiguous claim) qualifies as annual labor 
for&nbsp;&nbsp;that&nbsp;&nbsp;claim,&nbsp;&nbsp;is whether&nbsp;&nbsp;the 
work&nbsp;&nbsp;was done in good faith for the development&nbsp;&nbsp;of 
the&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;claim.</font></font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.4pt 0pt 0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 11pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0.05pt 6.55pt 0pt 6.3pt;line-height:103.75%;text-
indent:36pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none

<font style="display:inline;font-size:11pt;">The question of
whether group assessment work performed in any year actually benefited each and 
every claim listed in an affidavit of annual labor is necessarily based upon 
facts not of record. In preparing this report, we have assumed that all reported
assessment work, including all group assessment work, was performed in good 
faith for the benefit of each of the Subject Claims.</font>
